function initPage() {
	
	if (isNotNull(message)) {
		popTip(message);
	}
	if(ikeyAuthEnable=='Y'){
		showIkeyCode();
	}else if(showImgCodeThreshold==0){
		showRandCode();
	}
	if (showResetPwdLink == '#') {
		$(".wjmm").css('display', 'none');
	}
	if (showFindAccountLink == '#') {
		$(".wjzh").css('display', 'none');
	}
	if (showSelfServiceLink == '#') {
		$(".zzfw").css('display', 'none');
	}
	if (showModifyPwdLink == '#') {
		$(".xgmm").css('display', 'none');
		$("#modifyPwdBtn").css('display', 'none');
	}else{
		 $('#modifyPwdBtn').click(function(event) {
			 openWin('https://pacas.pa18.com/cas/umChangeAgentPartnerPwd','444','520')
			 $('#myModal').modal('hide');
		 });
	}
	
	var placeholder = '请输入UM密码';
	if(adAuthEnable=='true'){
		placeholder = '请输入开机密码';
	}
	$('#password').attr('placeholder',placeholder);
}
